Thank you guys for bringing back real R&Bâ€¦this is what we need during these crazy times!
End of September till October was rough for me. To numerate:  1. Lost my grandmother, 79, after being nursed by his husband, 84, for 2 years straight on his own (with me ofc, but without my mom/their daughter and other sons). He had to figure out all on his own to make ends meet so that he could keep her alive for long.  2. Grandfather contracted COVID a week after her death, which became a lot worse considering he already had pneumonia prior. Won the battle against COVID but passed away just a week after / 30 days after her wife left us. He didn't have any time to mourn properly for lola's death.  3. I myself got the virus and got hospitalized -- wasn't even able to be there for him when he got rushed to the ER for the last time.  4. Uncle from the other side of my family passed away in his sleep.  5. Pet dog died. He was just 3 weeks old.  During all of these, I just let my emotions get pushed to one side by letting myself be occupied with things I find in the internet. I found their new album because of it in hopes that all the hype around their  music would help further in being distracted, but the lyricism here in this very song broke the chain deep down inside me. It perfectly narrated what I'm going through, what I wish I could do. I just miss them a lot, but all I can do is put on a smile. ğŸ˜­ğŸ˜­  Now I have this on loop because that's all I can really do now -- to let all the emotions run rampant, in hopes that overtime all of these would make sense. I dont even know what I'm aiming for, I just want to be lonely for them.

Yeee
This is hands down my stand out track. We get Enchantment and Delfonics vibes here in spades. Most men can relate to being broken-hearted yet doing all they can to hide what is really going on inside. This track with its sad and somehow delightful chords pull on ones heartstrings as both Anderson.Paak and Bruno Mars croon in authentic vulnerable fashion. The production is layered and voluminous. You can tell a lot of time and effort went into the creation of this masterpiece. Songwriter extraordinaire Babyface is listed as one of the background vocalist, and my ears can't argue with that. This track builds like a hurricane gaining strength in the Gulf of Mexico. AP gives us an incredible raspy Sugerfoot (Ohio Players) type vibe here, and BM is again stellar crooning powerful high notes like Bobby De'Barge (Switch) in some instances here. Musically this is an extraordinarily soul touching song. The drum work by AP toward the latter part of this song is bananas. This is no doubt my favorite on the album - just remarkable attention to detail production-wise.

Over One Million Signatures Against Forced Organ Harvesting Doctors Against Forced Organ Harvesting (DAFOH) started a global petition in 2013 to oppose the forced organ harvesting in China. Within 5 months, over 1.5 million signatures were collected in more than 50 nations. They were submitted to the Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights (OHCHR), urging immediate action to stop the forced organ harvesting of Falun Gong practitioners in China.   In an announcement on June 14, the United Nations Human Rights Council stated that the accusations against the CCP for harvesting organs from detained Falun Gong practitioners, Uyghurs, Tibetans, Muslims, and Christians are shocking.

I gotta say, it is a pleasure to be musically tortured the way Silk Sonic does so;  the arrangements, compositions, song writing, phrasing, (and of course dancing) is incomparable and out of this world!    What I appreciate most is that they are raising the bar to how we think of albums,  that they are an audible storyboard for artists.  Instant gratification keeps us feeding on single track soundbites rather than trying to digest a whole audio voyage like these cats are taking us on.  I like that they are challenging other artists to approach their music in that fashion.    Other artists like Mayer Hawthorne and Tuxedo have been diving into the Motown/RnB revitalization for several years now and Silk Sonic is giving their rendition and giving song writing/composition new meaning.  Much Mahalo to Anderson and Bruno for the gift of their musical aloha;  I don't think I can do enough to deserve their musicianship.... (cue riotous standing ovation)
